\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{p\_Equalizer\_overview()}{p\_Equalizer\_overview()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void p\+\_\+\+Equalizer\+\_\+overview (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



this function edits the ON/\+OFF settings of the Equalizer, the parameters and sources have to be edited on another page or you can switch to the next effect
